beforeAll(async () => {
  container = await new GenericContainer('localstack/localstack', '0.12.2')
    .withEnv('SERVICES', 'dynamodb')
    .withEnv('LOCALSTACK_HOSTNAME', 'localhost')
    .withEnv('EDGE_PORT', '4569')
    .withEnv('DEFAULT_REGION', 'us-east-1')
    .withEnv('DEBUG', 'true')
    .withEnv('LAMBDA_EXECUTOR', 'local')
    .withEnv('LAMBDA_REMOTE_DOCKER', 'false')
    .withExposedPorts(4569)
    .start()

  process.env.AWS_REGION = 'us-east-1'
  process.env.AWS_ENDPOINT = `http://localhost:${container.getMappedPort(
    4569,
  )}`
  databaseContext = new DatabaseContext().docClient()
})

afterAll(async () => {
  await container.stop()

const path = require("path");
const redis = require("async-redis");
const { DockerComposeEnvironment } = require("testcontainers");

(async () => {
  const composeFilePath = path.resolve(__dirname, "dir-containing-docker-compose-yml");
  const composeFile = "docker-compose.yml"
  const environment = await new DockerComposeEnvironment(composeFilePath, composeFile).up();
  const container = environment.getContainer("redis_1");
  
  const redisClient = redis.createClient(
    container.getMappedPort(6379),
    container.getContainerIpAddress(),
  );
  await redisClient.quit();
  await environment.down();
})();
